tc4h9o2 + phch2ooj = tc4h9o + phch2oj + o2  1.40E+16 -1.61 1860.

o2 + c*cc*cc = ho2 + c*cc*ccj  4.00E+12 0 39900 !prf mech for abstraction from C*CC
